<script data-pagespeed-no-defer="" pagespeed_no_defer="">
        (function() {
            function getExperimentStates(filter) {
                return window.optimizely.get('state').getExperimentStates(filter);
            }

            function isExperimentActive(id) {
                return Object.keys(getExperimentStates({ isActive: true })).includes(id);
            }

            // Array of the experiments' state by experiment id
            var experimentsPromises = {};
            var experimentIds = new Set();

            function getExperimentObj(experimentId) {
                experimentIds.add(experimentId);
                var currentExperimentPromise = experimentsPromises[experimentId];
                if (currentExperimentPromise == null) {
                    var outsideResolve, outsideReject;
                    var experimentPromise = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                        outsideResolve = resolve;
                    });
                    var experimentPromiseObj = {
                        _resolve: outsideResolve,
                        promise: experimentPromise
                    };
                    experimentsPromises[experimentId] = experimentPromiseObj;
                    return experimentPromiseObj;
                } else {
                    return currentExperimentPromise;
                }
            }

            var experiments = {
                get: function(experimentId) {
                    window.optimizelyReady.then(function(_) {
                        var experimentState = getExperimentStates()[experimentId];
                        if (experimentState && !experimentState.isActive) {
                            getExperimentObj(experimentId)._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is not active' });
                        } else if (!experimentState) {
                            getExperimentObj(experimentId)._resolve({
                                error: 'Experiment id not found: check if correct'
                            });
                        }
                    });
                    return getExperimentObj(experimentId).promise;
                }
            };

            window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];

            window.optimizely.push({
                type: 'addListener',
                filter: {
                    type: 'lifecycle',
                    name: 'campaignDecided'
                },
                handler: function(event) {
                    var id = event.data.decision.experimentId;
                    var experimentObj = getExperimentObj(id);
                    var experimentData = getExperimentStates()[id];
                    if (experimentData && experimentData.isActive) {
                        if (experimentData.isInExperimentHoldback) {
                            experimentObj._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is in holdback' });
                        } else {
                            experimentObj._resolve(event.data);
                        }
                    } else {
                        experimentObj._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is not active' });
                    }
                }
            });
            window.optimizelyHelper = { get: experiments.get.bind(experiments) };
            window.optimizelyReady = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                window.optimizely.push({
                    type: 'addListener',
                    filter: {
                        type: 'lifecycle',
                        name: 'initialized'
                    },
                    handler: function() {
                        var state = window.optimizely.get('state');
                        resolve({ optimizely: window.optimizely, state: state, variationMap: state.getVariationMap() });
                    }
                });
                var script = document.createElement('script');
                var ref = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                script.onerror = reject;
                script.src = 'https://cdn.optimizely.com/js/8387223727.js';
                ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
            });

            var as24optimizely = Object.assign(Object.create(HTMLElement.prototype), {
                attachedCallback: function() {
                    window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
                    var action = this.getAttribute('action');
                    if (action == 'push') {
                        var payload = JSON.parse(this.getAttribute('payload'));
                        window.optimizely.push(payload);
                    }
                }
            });
            document.registerElement('as24-optimizely', { prototype: as24optimizely });
        })();
    </script>
